initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">NAND 数据不是天然干净地读出来的，而是被 ECC 救回来的。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: initial;"><span leaf="">主机发来一个 read 命令，SSD 从 NAND 里读出一页数据。 这份数据不是百分百正确的，里面可能已经有很多 bit 读错了。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这时候 ECC 出场。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei rgb(0, 0, 0);margin-top: 0px;"><span leaf="">Read Retry</span></strong><span leaf="">。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这页数据坏了。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但更准确的说法是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">在当前这次读取结果下，错误 bit 太多，ECC 暂时救不回来。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: bold;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);margin-top: 0px;"><span leaf="">当前这次读取结果。</span></strong></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">NAND 读数据不是像硬盘那样，把某个磁区里的数据直接“拿出来”。NAND cell 里真正存的是电压状态。读数据时，SSD 要根据这些电压状态判断它属于哪个逻辑状态。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">换句话说，NAND read 的本质不是“取出答案”，而是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">根据电压位置，判断这个 cell 更像哪个状态。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">如果判断电压选得不合适，就可能把一些本来还能分清的 cell 判错。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">于是 raw bit error 增加。 ECC 看到的错误变多。 如果错误多到超过 ECC 能力，ECC 就失败。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但这并不一定代表 cell 里的信息已经完全消失。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, leaf="">这次读的时候，判断线放错了位置。</span></p></blockquote><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: leaf="">Read Retry 可以把数据救回来。但如果某个 block / SPB 里的数据经常要靠 Read Retry 才能读出来，这不是一个好信号。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: 控制器不会每次都等到读失败才临时抢救。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">如果某个 block / SPB 经常需要 Read Retry 才能读出来，SSD 可能不会继续让数据留在原地。控制器会趁数据还能被 ECC 救回来时，把它搬到新的位置。这个过程在固件实现里可能表现为一次 recycle 或数据刷新。它和普通 GC 很像，但目的不是单纯腾空间，而是降低后续读失败的风险。</span></p></blockquote><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: leaf="">：</span></span></code></span></span></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;margin-top: 6px !important;margin-right: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;margin-left: 0px;padding: 0px 0px 0px 1em;background: rgb(45, 45, 45);list-style-type: decimal;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px !important;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);margin-top: 0px;display: block;word-break: inherit !important;line-height: 22px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px !important;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);margin-top: 0px;line-height: 22px;display: block;word-break: inherit !important;"><code style="white-space:pre-wrap;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;padding: 0px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;font-family: inherit !important;display: flex;overflow: 20px;white-space: inherit !important;font-family: consolas, menlo, courier, &quot;monospace&quot;, &quot;Microsoft Yahei&quot; !important;"><span leaf="">十六个状态，间隔更小，判断更难</span></span></code></span></span></li></ol></pre><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: initial;"><span leaf="">电压窗口越窄，对 read reference voltage 越敏感。一点点漂移，就可能让默认判断线不再合适。所以越是高密度 NAND，越需要更复杂的读恢复机制。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这也是现代 SSD 的本质矛盾：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 必须越来越聪明。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, 是另一层。 后面还有 read calibration、soft decode、风险数据搬迁 等一整套机制。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none leaf="">读失败了，再读一遍。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: SSD 读恢复的核心路径。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, SSD 内部，可能已经经历了：</span></p><pre style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 8px 0px 6px;font-family: consolas, menlo, courier, &quot;monospace&quot;, &quot;Microsoft Yahei&quot;
